+ evaluation 层

现在最自然的下一步就是你问的这个：

# 一、什么是“简单预测结果格式”
它本质上就是：

**模型或 baseline 对每道题给出的答案，保存成一个统一文件**

因为后面不管你是：

+ OCR baseline
+ 规则 baseline
+ 训练后的模型
+ 以后 ChartQA 分支

它们最后都要输出“预测答案”。  
所以你现在要做的是：**先把预测结果的保存/加载格式统一好。**

---

## 最推荐的格式
我建议你先用 **JSON 列表**，每一项就是一道题的预测结果。

长这样：

```json
[
  {
    "question_id": "337",
    "prediction": "1/8/93"
  },
  {
    "question_id": "338",
    "prediction": "P. Carter"
  }
]
```

这是最简单、最好调试、最好和 evaluator 对接的格式。

---

## 为什么这样设计最好理解
因为每一项就只回答两个问题：

1. **这是哪一道题？**
    - `question_id`
2. **我预测的答案是什么？**
    - `prediction`

以后如果你想多存一点东西，也可以加：

+ `meta`
+ `confidence`
+ `method`

例如：

```json
[
  {
    "question_id": "337",
    "prediction": "1/8/93",
    "meta": {
      "method": "ocr_baseline"
    }
  }
]
```

但第一版先不要复杂化。

---

# 二、你现在应该新建什么文件
我建议你现在加这两个文件：

1. `src/mm_docvqa/inference/prediction_io.py`
2. `tests/test_prediction_io.py`

它们的作用分别是：

## `prediction_io.py`
负责：

+ 把预测结果保存成 JSON
+ 从 JSON 再读回来
+ 转成你 evaluator 能直接使用的 `PredictionRecord`

## `test_prediction_io.py`
负责：

+ 测保存功能没写错
+ 测加载功能没写错
+ 测 JSON 结构符合预期

---

# 三、直接给你代码
---

## 1）`src/mm_docvqa/inference/prediction_io.py`
```python
from __future__ import annotations

import json
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any

from mm_docvqa.domain.schemas import PredictionRecord


def prediction_record_to_dict(record: PredictionRecord) -> dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Convert one PredictionRecord into a plain JSON-serializable dict.
    """
    return {
        "question_id": record.question_id,
        "prediction": record.prediction,
        "meta": record.meta,
    }


def prediction_dict_to_record(data: dict[str, Any]) -> PredictionRecord:
    """
    Convert one plain dict into PredictionRecord.
    """
    return PredictionRecord(
        question_id=str(data["question_id"]),
        prediction=str(data["prediction"]),
        dataset_name="docvqa",
        meta=data.get("meta", {}),
    )


def save_predictions(
    predictions: list[PredictionRecord],
    output_path: str | Path,
) -> Path:
    """
    Save predictions to a JSON file.

    Output format:
    [
      {
        "question_id": "337",
        "prediction": "1/8/93",
        "meta": {}
      },
      ...
    ]
    """
    output_path = Path(output_path)
    output_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    payload = [prediction_record_to_dict(record) for record in predictions]

    with output_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(payload, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)

    return output_path


def load_predictions(input_path: str | Path) -> list[PredictionRecord]:
    """
    Load predictions from a JSON file and return PredictionRecord objects.
    """
    input_path = Path(input_path)
    with input_path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        payload = json.load(f)

    if not isinstance(payload, list):
        raise ValueError("Prediction file must contain a list of predictions")

    return [prediction_dict_to_record(item) for item in payload]


def build_prediction_records_from_pairs(
    pairs: list[tuple[str, str]],
) -> list[PredictionRecord]:
    """
    Build prediction records from (question_id, prediction) pairs.
    """
    return [
        PredictionRecord(
            question_id=question_id,
            prediction=prediction,
            dataset_name="docvqa",
        )
        for question_id, prediction in pairs
    ]
```

---

## 2）`tests/test_prediction_io.py`
```python
import json
from pathlib import Path

from mm_docvqa.domain.schemas import PredictionRecord
from mm_docvqa.inference.prediction_io import (
    build_prediction_records_from_pairs,
    load_predictions,
    prediction_dict_to_record,
    prediction_record_to_dict,
    save_predictions,
)


def test_prediction_record_to_dict() -> None:
    record = PredictionRecord(
        question_id="337",
        prediction="1/8/93",
        dataset_name="docvqa",
        meta={"method": "ocr_baseline"},
    )

    data = prediction_record_to_dict(record)

    assert data["question_id"] == "337"
    assert data["prediction"] == "1/8/93"
    assert data["meta"]["method"] == "ocr_baseline"


def test_prediction_dict_to_record() -> None:
    data = {
        "question_id": "338",
        "prediction": "P. Carter",
        "meta": {"method": "ocr_baseline"},
    }

    record = prediction_dict_to_record(data)

    assert record.question_id == "338"
    assert record.prediction == "P. Carter"
    assert record.meta["method"] == "ocr_baseline"


def test_save_and_load_predictions(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
    predictions = [
        PredictionRecord(question_id="337", prediction="1/8/93", dataset_name="docvqa"),
        PredictionRecord(question_id="338", prediction="P. Carter", dataset_name="docvqa"),
    ]

    output_path = tmp_path / "predictions.json"
    save_predictions(predictions, output_path)

    assert output_path.exists()

    loaded = load_predictions(output_path)

    assert len(loaded) == 2
    assert loaded[0].question_id == "337"
    assert loaded[0].prediction == "1/8/93"
    assert loaded[1].question_id == "338"
    assert loaded[1].prediction == "P. Carter"


def test_saved_json_structure(tmp_path: Path) -> None:
    predictions = [
        PredictionRecord(question_id="337", prediction="1/8/93", dataset_name="docvqa"),
    ]

    output_path = tmp_path / "predictions.json"
    save_predictions(predictions, output_path)

    data = json.loads(output_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))

    assert isinstance(data, list)
    assert data[0]["question_id"] == "337"
    assert data[0]["prediction"] == "1/8/93"


def test_build_prediction_records_from_pairs() -> None:
    pairs = [
        ("337", "1/8/93"),
        ("338", "P. Carter"),
    ]

    records = build_prediction_records_from_pairs(pairs)

    assert len(records) == 2
    assert records[0].question_id == "337"
    assert records[1].prediction == "P. Carter"
```

---

# 四、你现在怎么操作
先把这两个文件放进去，然后运行：

```bash
pytest tests/test_prediction_io.py
pytest
```

---

# 五、为什么这一步很重要
这一步做完以后，你的项目就多了一条完整链路：

+ `DocumentSample`：真实题目
+ `PredictionRecord`：模型预测
+ `save_predictions(...)`：保存结果
+ `load_predictions(...)`：读回结果
+ `evaluate_predictions(...)`：计算指标

这意味着：

你已经具备了“预测 -> 保存 -> 读取 -> 打分”的闭环

也就是说，后面 baseline 只要能生成答案，就能立刻接上整个评测系统。

---

# 六、接下来该怎么操作
你现在最适合的顺序是这个：

## 第一步
先把上面两个文件写好，跑测试。

## 第二步
做一个最小“假预测”脚本，验证整条链路真的通了。

比如新建一个小脚本：

`scripts/debug_eval_pipeline.py`

作用是：

+ 手工造 2 条 `PredictionRecord`
+ 调 `save_predictions`
+ 再 `load_predictions`
+ 再 `evaluate_predictions`

这样你会非常清楚整条链路怎么跑。

不过这一步可以稍后做，不是必须先写。

## 第三步
正式进入你第一个 baseline：

### 下一批文件
1. `src/mm_docvqa/baselines/ocr_retrieval.py`
2. `src/mm_docvqa/inference/predict_docvqa_baseline.py`
3. `tests/test_baseline_docvqa.py`

---

# 七、这三个下一批文件分别做什么
## `ocr_retrieval.py`
做最简单的基线逻辑：

+ 输入：question + OCR text
+ 处理：按规则从 OCR 文本里找可能答案
+ 输出：预测字符串

注意：  
第一版 baseline 不追求厉害，只追求“完整可跑”。

---

## `predict_docvqa_baseline.py`
这个脚本做的是：

+ 读取真实 DocVQA 数据
+ 读取每条样本对应的 OCR
+ 调 `ocr_retrieval.py`
+ 为每道题生成 `PredictionRecord`
+ 保存成 JSON

---

## `test_baseline_docvqa.py`
这个文件测试的是：

+ baseline 函数至少能输出字符串
+ 空 OCR / 空问题时不会崩
+ 一些非常简单的 toy case 有合理输出

---

# 八、你现在最推荐的下一步
你刚刚问“接下来该怎么操作”，我的建议非常明确：

### 现在先做：
+ `prediction_io.py`
+ `test_prediction_io.py`

### 然后立刻进入：
+ `ocr_retrieval.py`
+ `predict_docvqa_baseline.py`
+ `test_baseline_docvqa.py`

也就是开始你项目的**第一个真正 baseline**。

你把 `test_prediction_io.py` 跑过以后，下一条我就直接继续给你写 baseline 这 3 个文件。



# 指令运行后并没有报错，可以为我写接下来的代码吗？
可以，下面我直接把**第一版 baseline** 的 3 个核心文件给你，并顺带把它们的功能讲清楚。

这一步的目标不是“很强”，而是：

+ 能从 **question + OCR** 里产出一个答案
+ 能把答案保存成 prediction 文件
+ 能直接接上你已经写好的 evaluator 跑分

也就是说，这一步做完后，你就有了项目里**第一个真正可跑的 baseline**。

---

# 这一批文件分别做什么
## 1. `src/mm_docvqa/baselines/ocr_retrieval.py`
这是 baseline 的“核心算法”文件。

它做的事情是：

+ 读取问题 `question`
+ 读取 OCR 提取出来的整页文字 `ocr_page`
+ 从 OCR 的每一行里挑出“最可能包含答案”的那一行
+ 再从这一行里提取答案

你可以把它理解成：

先“找答案最可能在哪一行”，再“从这行里抠出答案”。

---

## 2. `src/mm_docvqa/inference/predict_docvqa_baseline.py`
这是 baseline 的“执行脚本”。

它做的事情是：

+ 读取真实 DocVQA 数据
+ 读取每条样本对应的 OCR 文件
+ 调用 `ocr_retrieval.py`
+ 为每道题生成一个预测答案
+ 保存成 JSON
+ 如果有标准答案（train/val），还会自动跑评测

你可以把它理解成：

把 baseline 真正跑在真实数据上。

---

## 3. `tests/test_baseline_docvqa.py`
这是 baseline 的测试文件。

它做的事情是：

+ 用小样本验证 baseline 不会崩
+ 验证它至少能处理一些最简单的情况
+ 确保以后你重构代码时，不会把 baseline 基本逻辑搞坏

---

# 现在直接给你代码
---

## 1）`src/mm_docvqa/baselines/ocr_retrieval.py`
先确保有目录：

```plain
src/mm_docvqa/baselines/
```

如果没有，就建一个。  
同时建议顺手建一个空文件：

```plain
src/mm_docvqa/baselines/__init__.py
```

然后新建：

`src/mm_docvqa/baselines/ocr_retrieval.py`

```python
from __future__ import annotations

import re

from mm_docvqa.domain.schemas import OCRLine, OCRPage
from mm_docvqa.evaluation.normalize import normalize_text


STOPWORDS = {
    "what",
    "is",
    "the",
    "a",
    "an",
    "of",
    "in",
    "this",
    "that",
    "who",
    "whose",
    "which",
    "when",
    "where",
    "how",
    "many",
    "mentioned",
    "letter",
    "document",
    "name",
    "given",
    "does",
    "do",
    "to",
    "for",
    "on",
    "and",
    "or",
    "are",
    "be",
    "cc",
}


DATE_PATTERNS = [
    r"\b\d{1,2}/\d{1,2}/\d{2,4}\b",
    r"\b\d{1,2}-\d{1,2}-\d{2,4}\b",
    r"\b(?:jan|feb|mar|apr|may|jun|jul|aug|sep|sept|oct|nov|dec)[a-z]*\s+\d{1,2},?\s+\d{2,4}\b",
]


def simple_tokenize(text: str) -> list[str]:
    """
    Tokenize normalized text into alphanumeric tokens.
    """
    text = normalize_text(text)
    return re.findall(r"[a-z0-9]+", text)


def question_keywords(question: str) -> set[str]:
    """
    Keep only more meaningful question keywords.
    """
    tokens = simple_tokenize(question)
    return {token for token in tokens if token not in STOPWORDS and len(token) > 1}


def question_hints(question: str) -> list[str]:
    """
    Heuristic hints from question intent.
    These hints help us prefer OCR lines containing likely labels.
    """
    q = normalize_text(question)
    hints: list[str] = []

    if "date" in q:
        hints.extend(["date", "dated"])
    if "subject" in q:
        hints.extend(["subject", "re:"])
    if "contact person" in q or "contact" in q:
        hints.extend(["contact", "attention", "attn"])
    if "signature" in q or "whose signature" in q:
        hints.extend(["signature", "signed"])
    if "cc" in q:
        hints.append("cc")
    if "corporation" in q or "letterhead" in q or "company" in q:
        hints.extend(["company", "corporation", "inc", "co"])
    if "name" in q:
        hints.append("name")

    return hints


def extract_after_colon(text: str) -> str:
    """
    Extract the text after the first colon if present.
    Example:
    'Subject: Review of existing ideas' -> 'Review of existing ideas'
    """
    if ":" not in text:
        return ""
    parts = text.split(":", maxsplit=1)
    if len(parts) != 2:
        return ""
    return parts[1].strip()


def find_first_date(text: str) -> str:
    """
    Return the first date-like substring if found, otherwise empty string.
    """
    normalized = normalize_text(text)
    for pattern in DATE_PATTERNS:
        match = re.search(pattern, normalized, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        if match:
            return match.group(0)
    return ""


def score_line(question: str, line: OCRLine) -> float:
    """
    Heuristic score for how likely an OCR line contains the answer.
    """
    q_keywords = question_keywords(question)
    hints = question_hints(question)

    line_norm = normalize_text(line.text)
    line_tokens = set(simple_tokenize(line.text))

    if not line_norm:
        return -1.0

    score = 0.0

    # Basic keyword overlap
    score += float(len(q_keywords & line_tokens))

    # Hint bonus if line contains likely label words
    for hint in hints:
        if hint in line_norm:
            score += 2.0

    # Colon bonus, because many forms use "Label: Value"
    if ":" in line.text:
        score += 0.5

    # Slight bonus for short lines: labels often appear in concise lines
    if len(line.text) < 80:
        score += 0.2

    return score


def select_best_line(question: str, ocr_page: OCRPage | None) -> OCRLine | None:
    """
    Select the highest-scoring OCR line for a question.
    """
    if ocr_page is None or not ocr_page.lines:
        return None

    scored_lines = [(score_line(question, line), line) for line in ocr_page.lines]
    scored_lines.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)

    best_score, best_line = scored_lines[0]
    if best_score < 0:
        return None
    return best_line


def extract_answer_from_line(question: str, line_text: str, page_text: str = "") -> str:
    """
    Turn one likely OCR line into a final answer string.
    """
    q = normalize_text(question)
    line_text = line_text.strip()

    if not line_text:
        return ""

    # Date question -> prefer date pattern
    if "date" in q:
        date = find_first_date(line_text)
        if date:
            return date
        if page_text:
            date = find_first_date(page_text)
            if date:
                return date

    # Common label-value format
    value_after_colon = extract_after_colon(line_text)
    if value_after_colon:
        return value_after_colon

    # Fallback: return the whole line
    return line_text


def predict_answer(question: str, ocr_page: OCRPage | None) -> str:
    """
    Main baseline entry point.

    Strategy:
    1. Select the best OCR line using keyword + hint overlap.
    2. Extract answer from that line.
    3. If nothing works, return empty string.
    """
    if ocr_page is None:
        return ""

    best_line = select_best_line(question, ocr_page)
    if best_line is None:
        return ""

    return extract_answer_from_line(
        question=question,
        line_text=best_line.text,
        page_text=ocr_page.full_text(),
    )
```

---

## 2）`src/mm_docvqa/inference/predict_docvqa_baseline.py`
新建文件：

`src/mm_docvqa/inference/predict_docvqa_baseline.py`

```python
from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import json
from pathlib import Path

from mm_docvqa.baselines.ocr_retrieval import predict_answer
from mm_docvqa.data.loader import (
    DocVQAPaths,
    get_default_docvqa_qas_file,
    load_docvqa_manifest_with_assets,
    load_docvqa_ocr_page,
)
from mm_docvqa.domain.schemas import PredictionRecord
from mm_docvqa.evaluation.evaluator import evaluate_predictions
from mm_docvqa.inference.prediction_io import save_predictions


def parse_args() -> argparse.Namespace:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Run a simple OCR baseline on DocVQA.")
    parser.add_argument(
        "--docvqa-root",
        type=str,
        default="datasets/docvqa",
        help="Root directory of the downloaded DocVQA dataset.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--split",
        type=str,
        default="val",
        choices=["train", "val", "test"],
        help="Dataset split to run on.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--limit",
        type=int,
        default=None,
        help="Optional number of samples to process.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--output-path",
        type=str,
        default=None,
        help="Where to save predictions JSON.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--save-metrics",
        action="store_true",
        help="If set, also save evaluation summary JSON for train/val.",
    )
    return parser.parse_args()


def main() -> None:
    args = parse_args()

    docvqa_root = Path(args.docvqa_root)
    paths = DocVQAPaths.from_root(docvqa_root)

    qas_path = get_default_docvqa_qas_file(paths.qas_dir, args.split)

    manifest = load_docvqa_manifest_with_assets(
        qas_json_path=qas_path,
        images_dir=paths.images_dir,
        ocr_dir=paths.ocr_dir,
    )

    if args.limit is not None:
        manifest.samples = manifest.samples[: args.limit]

    if args.output_path is None:
        output_path = Path("outputs/preds") / f"docvqa_{args.split}_ocr_baseline.json"
    else:
        output_path = Path(args.output_path)

    predictions: list[PredictionRecord] = []
    ocr_cache = {}

    print("=" * 80)
    print("Running OCR baseline")
    print("split        :", args.split)
    print("num_samples  :", len(manifest.samples))
    print("qas_path     :", qas_path)
    print("output_path  :", output_path)
    print("=" * 80)

    for idx, sample in enumerate(manifest.samples):
        ocr_path = sample.meta.get("ocr_path", "")

        if ocr_path and ocr_path not in ocr_cache:
            ocr_file = Path(ocr_path)
            if ocr_file.exists():
                ocr_cache[ocr_path] = load_docvqa_ocr_page(ocr_file)
            else:
                ocr_cache[ocr_path] = None

        ocr_page = ocr_cache.get(ocr_path)
        prediction = predict_answer(sample.question, ocr_page)

        predictions.append(
            PredictionRecord(
                question_id=sample.question_id,
                prediction=prediction,
                dataset_name="docvqa",
                meta={
                    "method": "ocr_baseline_v1",
                    "ocr_path": ocr_path,
                },
            )
        )

        if idx < 3:
            print(f"[preview {idx}]")
            print("question   :", sample.question)
            print("gt_answers :", sample.answers)
            print("prediction :", prediction)
            print("-" * 80)

    save_predictions(predictions, output_path)
    print(f"Saved predictions to: {output_path}")

    if args.split != "test":
        summary = evaluate_predictions(manifest.samples, predictions)
        print("=" * 80)
        print("Evaluation summary")
        print(json.dumps(summary.to_dict(), indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))
        print("=" * 80)

        if args.save_metrics:
            metrics_path = output_path.with_name(output_path.stem + "_metrics.json")
            metrics_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            with metrics_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                json.dump(summary.to_dict(), f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
            print(f"Saved metrics to: {metrics_path}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

---

## 3）`tests/test_baseline_docvqa.py`
新建文件：

`tests/test_baseline_docvqa.py`

```python
from mm_docvqa.baselines.ocr_retrieval import (
    extract_after_colon,
    find_first_date,
    predict_answer,
    question_keywords,
    select_best_line,
)
from mm_docvqa.domain.schemas import BBox, OCRLine, OCRPage, OCRWord


def make_line(text: str) -> OCRLine:
    return OCRLine(
        text=text,
        bbox=BBox(0, 0, 100, 20),
        words=[OCRWord(text=token, bbox=BBox(0, 0, 10, 10)) for token in text.split()],
    )


def make_page(lines: list[str]) -> OCRPage:
    return OCRPage(
        page_no=1,
        width=1000,
        height=1400,
        unit="pixel",
        orientation=0.0,
        status="Succeeded",
        source="microsoft_ocr",
        lines=[make_line(text) for text in lines],
    )


def test_question_keywords() -> None:
    q = "what is the date mentioned in this letter?"
    keywords = question_keywords(q)
    assert "date" in keywords
    assert "what" not in keywords
    assert "this" not in keywords


def test_extract_after_colon() -> None:
    text = "Subject: Review of existing Brainstorming Ideas/483"
    value = extract_after_colon(text)
    assert value == "Review of existing Brainstorming Ideas/483"


def test_find_first_date() -> None:
    text = "Date: 1/8/93"
    assert find_first_date(text) == "1/8/93"


def test_select_best_line_for_subject_question() -> None:
    page = make_page(
        [
            "Confidential",
            "Date: 1/8/93",
            "Subject: Review of existing Brainstorming Ideas/483",
        ]
    )

    best_line = select_best_line("what is the subject of this letter?", page)
    assert best_line is not None
    assert "Subject" in best_line.text


def test_predict_answer_for_date_question() -> None:
    page = make_page(
        [
            "Confidential",
            "Date: 1/8/93",
            "RJRT PR APPROVAL",
        ]
    )

    prediction = predict_answer("what is the date mentioned in this letter?", page)
    assert prediction == "1/8/93"


def test_predict_answer_for_subject_question() -> None:
    page = make_page(
        [
            "Confidential",
            "Subject: Review of existing Brainstorming Ideas/483",
        ]
    )

    prediction = predict_answer("what is the subject of this letter?", page)
    assert prediction == "Review of existing Brainstorming Ideas/483"


def test_predict_answer_with_empty_ocr() -> None:
    assert predict_answer("what is the date?", None) == ""


def test_predict_answer_fallback_to_full_line() -> None:
    page = make_page(
        [
            "Brown & Williamson Tobacco Corporation",
            "Confidential",
        ]
    )

    prediction = predict_answer("Which corporation's letterhead is this?", page)
    assert prediction == "Brown & Williamson Tobacco Corporation"
```

---

# 现在你怎么操作
先把这 3 个文件放进去，然后运行：

```bash
pytest tests/test_baseline_docvqa.py
pytest
```

# 跑完结果如下，结下来该怎么办？

+ 自动评测

现在这组分数：

+ exact match = **0.02**
+ anls = **0.03**

说明的是：

**baseline v1 能跑，但规则太粗糙，几乎还没有真正理解文档问答。**

这很正常。第一版 baseline 的任务本来就不是“分数高”，而是“把闭环打通”。

---

## 先看你这 3 条预览，问题已经很明显了
### 第 1 条
问题是：

What is the ‘actual’ value per 1000, during the year 1975?

标准答案：  
`0.28`

预测：  
`1975`

这说明 baseline 目前的问题是：

+ 它抓到了问题里的关键词
+ 但没有理解“问的是数值，不是年份”
+ 它只是捞到了相关行里的一个显眼 token

也就是说，它现在更像“关键词命中”，不像“答案抽取”。

---

### 第 2 条
问题是：

What is name of university?

标准答案：  
`university of california / University of California / university of california, san diego`

预测：  
`UNIVERSITY OF CALIFORNIA, SAN DIEGO`

这条其实已经**接近正确**了。  
只是说明两件事：

1. baseline 并不是完全没用
2. 你的评测现在很严格，或者答案里存在多个可接受版本，而 baseline 没完全贴住标准答案集合

这类例子很适合后面做 error analysis。

---

### 第 3 条
问题是：

What is the name of the company?

标准答案：  
`ITC Limited`

预测：  
`ITC Limited REPORT AND ACCOUNTS 2013`

这说明 baseline 现在有个典型问题：

**它能找到对的那一行，但不会把答案从整行里切出来。**

这就是下一步最该优化的地方。

---

# 结论：你现在不要急着上训练模型
你现在最正确的下一步，不是立刻去写 LayoutLMv2 训练代码。  
而是先做两件事：

## 第一件：分析 baseline 错在哪
## 第二件：把 baseline 从 v1 提升到 v2
因为你现在已经有可运行系统了，接下来最值钱的是：

让你知道它为什么错，以及怎么改会变好。

这一步做完，你后面不管是继续优化规则，还是切到训练模型，都会更稳。

---

# 接下来按这个顺序做
---

## 第一步：写一个 baseline 分析脚本
你现在最该新增的文件是：

### 新文件
+ `scripts/analyze_docvqa_baseline.py`

### 这个脚本的功能
它负责：

1. 读取 `outputs/preds/docvqa_val_ocr_baseline.json`
2. 重新加载对应的 val samples
3. 调 evaluator 拿到每条题的结果
4. 把错误样例打印出来
5. 统计最常见错误类型

### 你要它至少输出什么
+ 总样本数
+ exact match / anls
+ 前 20 条错误样例：
    - question
    - gt answers
    - prediction
    - question_types
+ 哪些 question_types 最难

### 为什么这一步最重要
因为你现在不能凭感觉改规则。  
你必须先知道：

+ 日期类错得多不多
+ subject 类错得多不多
+ company / university / person name 类是不是更容易
+ chart-like numeric question 是不是几乎全错

---

## 第二步：把 baseline 升级成 v2
你现在的 baseline v1 核心逻辑是：

+ 选一条最相关的 OCR 行
+ 直接返回整行或简单截取

这太粗了。

### v2 要做的不是“大改架构”
而是做 4 个非常具体的增强：

### 1. 加入“答案类型意识”
根据问题类型判断答案更像什么：

+ date 类：优先找日期格式
+ company/university/person name 类：优先找短文本实体
+ subject 类：优先找 `Subject:` 后面的值
+ numeric/value 类：优先找数字/小数，而不是年份

像你第 1 条错误，就是典型的：

numeric question 被错误地返回成了 year

所以 v2 必须加：

+ 小数提取
+ 数值候选优先级

---

### 2. 不要只返回整行，要学会“切答案”
这是你第 3 条错误暴露出来的重点。

例如：

`ITC Limited REPORT AND ACCOUNTS 2013`

正确答案是：

`ITC Limited`

所以 v2 要加规则：

+ 遇到类似公司名/学校名问题时，优先截取前半段短实体
+ 去掉明显噪声尾巴：
    - `REPORT AND ACCOUNTS`
    - 年份
    - 多余说明词

这一步会明显提升 name/entity 类问题。

---

### 3. 不只看一行，改成 top-k 候选行
现在 v1 是“选最优一行，然后直接抽答案”。

v2 建议改成：

+ 先选 top-3 行
+ 再从这 3 行里选最像答案的 span

因为很多文档问答里：

+ 问题关键词在一行
+ 真正答案在下一行或同区域另一行

这会让规则更稳一些。

---

### 4. 利用 `question_types`
你真实数据里已经有：

+ `handwritten`
+ `form`
+ `layout`

这个字段现在不能浪费。

比如：

+ `layout` 类问题，更适合用 label/value 规则
+ `form` 类问题，冒号后取值可能更有效

这能让 baseline 开始有一点“任务感”。

---

# 第三步：把 baseline 跑大一点
你现在只跑了 50 条，这适合调试，但还不够稳定。

### 接下来建议你这样跑
先跑：

```bash
python -m mm_docvqa.inference.predict_docvqa_baseline \
  --docvqa-root datasets/docvqa \
  --split val \
  --limit 300 \
  --save-metrics
```

然后再跑：

```bash
python -m mm_docvqa.inference.predict_docvqa_baseline \
  --docvqa-root datasets/docvqa \
  --split val \
  --limit 1000 \
  --save-metrics
```

这样你才能知道：

+ 50 条的结果是不是偶然
+ baseline 在更大样本下到底表现如何

---

# 第四步：把实验记录写起来
现在你已经开始有“可对比实验”了，必须记下来。

### 现在就新建
+ `docs/experiments.md`

### 里面至少写：
+ baseline 名称：`ocr_baseline_v1`
+ 运行命令
+ 样本数

+ 你观察到的问题

这个文档以后：

+ 写 README
+ 写简历
+ 准备面试  
都会非常有用。

# 帮我写接下来的代码内容，并分析下一步该做什么？
可以。你现在最该补的代码，就是**baseline 分析脚本**。  
它的作用不是训练，也不是改模型，而是帮你回答这几个很关键的问题：

1. 现在这个 baseline 到底错在哪
2. 哪些 `question_types` 最难
3. 错误是不是集中在：
    - 数值题
    - 日期题
    - subject 类题
    - company / university / name 类题
4. 接下来该优先改哪几条规则

---

# 一、现在先新增这个文件
新建：

`src/mm_docvqa/evaluation/analysis.py`

这个文件负责做“按 question_types 聚合”的分析函数，后面的脚本会用它。

```python
from __future__ import annotations

from collections import defaultdict
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Any

from mm_docvqa.domain.schemas import DocumentSample
from mm_docvqa.evaluation.evaluator import SampleEvalResult


@dataclass(slots=True)
class GroupMetric:
    group_name: str
    n_samples: int
    exact_match: float
    anls: float

    def to_dict(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "group_name": self.group_name,
            "n_samples": self.n_samples,
            "exact_match": self.exact_match,
            "anls": self.anls,
        }


@dataclass(slots=True)
class ErrorCase:
    question_id: str
    question: str
    answers: list[str]
    prediction: str
    exact_match: float
    anls: float
    question_types: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    image_path: str = ""
    ocr_path: str = ""

    def to_dict(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "question_id": self.question_id,
            "question": self.question,
            "answers": self.answers,
            "prediction": self.prediction,
            "exact_match": self.exact_match,
            "anls": self.anls,
            "question_types": self.question_types,
            "image_path": self.image_path,
            "ocr_path": self.ocr_path,
        }


def group_results_by_question_type(
    samples: list[DocumentSample],
    per_sample_results: list[SampleEvalResult],
) -> list[GroupMetric]:
    """
    Aggregate metrics by question_types.

    One sample may belong to multiple question types, so it contributes to each type.
    """
    if len(samples) != len(per_sample_results):
        raise ValueError("samples and per_sample_results must have the same length")

    bucket_em: dict[str, float] = defaultdict(float)
    bucket_anls: dict[str, float] = defaultdict(float)
    bucket_count: dict[str, int] = defaultdict(int)

    for sample, result in zip(samples, per_sample_results):
        q_types = sample.question_types or ["unknown"]
        for q_type in q_types:
            bucket_em[q_type] += result.exact_match
            bucket_anls[q_type] += result.anls
            bucket_count[q_type] += 1

    metrics: list[GroupMetric] = []
    for q_type in sorted(bucket_count.keys()):
        n = bucket_count[q_type]
        metrics.append(
            GroupMetric(
                group_name=q_type,
                n_samples=n,
                exact_match=bucket_em[q_type] / n if n else 0.0,
                anls=bucket_anls[q_type] / n if n else 0.0,
            )
        )

    return metrics


def collect_error_cases(
    samples: list[DocumentSample],
    per_sample_results: list[SampleEvalResult],
    max_cases: int | None = None,
) -> list[ErrorCase]:
    """
    Collect error cases where exact match < 1.0.
    """
    if len(samples) != len(per_sample_results):
        raise ValueError("samples and per_sample_results must have the same length")

    error_cases: list[ErrorCase] = []

    for sample, result in zip(samples, per_sample_results):
        if result.exact_match >= 1.0:
            continue

        error_cases.append(
            ErrorCase(
                question_id=sample.question_id,
                question=sample.question,
                answers=sample.answers,
                prediction=result.prediction,
                exact_match=result.exact_match,
                anls=result.anls,
                question_types=sample.question_types,
                image_path=sample.image_path,
                ocr_path=str(sample.meta.get("ocr_path", "")),
            )
        )

    error_cases.sort(key=lambda x: (x.exact_match, x.anls))
    if max_cases is not None:
        return error_cases[:max_cases]
    return error_cases
```

---

# 二、再新增这个脚本
新建：

`scripts/analyze_docvqa_baseline.py`

这个脚本会：

+ 读取 val 样本
+ 读取你已经保存好的 prediction 文件
+ 重新做评测
+ 打印总体分数
+ 打印按 `question_types` 的分组结果
+ 打印前若干条错误样例
+ 可选保存分析结果到 JSON

```python
from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import json
from pathlib import Path

from mm_docvqa.data.loader import (
    DocVQAPaths,
    get_default_docvqa_qas_file,
    load_docvqa_manifest_with_assets,
)
from mm_docvqa.evaluation.analysis import collect_error_cases, group_results_by_question_type
from mm_docvqa.evaluation.evaluator import evaluate_predictions
from mm_docvqa.inference.prediction_io import load_predictions


def parse_args() -> argparse.Namespace:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Analyze DocVQA baseline predictions.")
    parser.add_argument(
        "--docvqa-root",
        type=str,
        default="datasets/docvqa",
        help="Root directory of the downloaded DocVQA dataset.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--split",
        type=str,
        default="val",
        choices=["train", "val", "test"],
        help="Dataset split to analyze.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--predictions-path",
        type=str,
        default="outputs/preds/docvqa_val_ocr_baseline.json",
        help="Path to saved predictions JSON.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--limit",
        type=int,
        default=None,
        help="Optional number of samples to analyze (must match prediction coverage).",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--num-errors",
        type=int,
        default=20,
        help="How many error cases to print.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--save-analysis",
        action="store_true",
        help="If set, save analysis summary JSON.",
    )
    return parser.parse_args()


def main() -> None:
    args = parse_args()

    docvqa_root = Path(args.docvqa_root)
    paths = DocVQAPaths.from_root(docvqa_root)
    qas_path = get_default_docvqa_qas_file(paths.qas_dir, args.split)

    manifest = load_docvqa_manifest_with_assets(
        qas_json_path=qas_path,
        images_dir=paths.images_dir,
        ocr_dir=paths.ocr_dir,
    )

    if args.limit is not None:
        manifest.samples = manifest.samples[: args.limit]

    predictions = load_predictions(args.predictions_path)
    summary = evaluate_predictions(manifest.samples, predictions)

    print("=" * 80)
    print("DocVQA baseline analysis")
    print("split             :", args.split)
    print("predictions_path  :", args.predictions_path)
    print("n_samples         :", summary.n_samples)
    print("n_predicted       :", summary.n_predicted)
    print("n_missing         :", summary.n_missing)
    print("exact_match       :", f"{summary.exact_match:.4f}")
    print("anls              :", f"{summary.anls:.4f}")
    print("=" * 80)

    grouped = group_results_by_question_type(manifest.samples, summary.per_sample)

    print("Metrics by question type")
    print("-" * 80)
    for item in grouped:
        print(
            f"{item.group_name:15s} "
            f"n={item.n_samples:5d} "
            f"EM={item.exact_match:.4f} "
            f"ANLS={item.anls:.4f}"
        )
    print("=" * 80)

    error_cases = collect_error_cases(
        manifest.samples,
        summary.per_sample,
        max_cases=args.num_errors,
    )

    print(f"Top {len(error_cases)} error cases")
    print("-" * 80)
    for idx, case in enumerate(error_cases):
        print(f"[Error {idx}]")
        print("question_id    :", case.question_id)
        print("question       :", case.question)
        print("answers        :", case.answers)
        print("prediction     :", case.prediction)
        print("exact_match    :", case.exact_match)
        print("anls           :", case.anls)
        print("question_types :", case.question_types)
        print("image_path     :", case.image_path)
        print("ocr_path       :", case.ocr_path)
        print("-" * 80)

    if args.save_analysis:
        analysis_path = Path(args.predictions_path).with_name(
            Path(args.predictions_path).stem + "_analysis.json"
        )
        payload = {
            "summary": summary.to_dict(),
            "grouped_metrics": [item.to_dict() for item in grouped],
            "error_cases": [case.to_dict() for case in error_cases],
        }
        analysis_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        with analysis_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            json.dump(payload, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        print(f"Saved analysis to: {analysis_path}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

---

# 三、建议再补一个测试文件
新建：

`tests/test_analysis.py`

这个测试文件不是必须现在就写很多，但建议先有最基本的，保证后面你改分析逻辑时不容易坏。

```python
from mm_docvqa.domain.schemas import DocumentSample
from mm_docvqa.evaluation.analysis import collect_error_cases, group_results_by_question_type
from mm_docvqa.evaluation.evaluator import SampleEvalResult


def test_group_results_by_question_type() -> None:
    samples = [
        DocumentSample(
            dataset_name="docvqa",
            split="val",
            question_id="1",
            question="what is the date?",
            image_path="a.png",
            answers=["1/8/93"],
            question_types=["form", "handwritten"],
        ),
        DocumentSample(
            dataset_name="docvqa",
            split="val",
            question_id="2",
            question="what is the company name?",
            image_path="b.png",
            answers=["ITC Limited"],
            question_types=["layout"],
        ),
    ]

    per_sample = [
        SampleEvalResult(
            question_id="1",
            question="what is the date?",
            prediction="1/8/93",
            answers=["1/8/93"],
            exact_match=1.0,
            anls=1.0,
        ),
        SampleEvalResult(
            question_id="2",
            question="what is the company name?",
            prediction="ITC Limited REPORT AND ACCOUNTS 2013",
            answers=["ITC Limited"],
            exact_match=0.0,
            anls=0.6,
        ),
    ]

    grouped = group_results_by_question_type(samples, per_sample)
    grouped_dict = {x.group_name: x for x in grouped}

    assert "form" in grouped_dict
    assert "handwritten" in grouped_dict
    assert "layout" in grouped_dict
    assert grouped_dict["form"].exact_match == 1.0
    assert grouped_dict["layout"].exact_match == 0.0


def test_collect_error_cases() -> None:
    samples = [
        DocumentSample(
            dataset_name="docvqa",
            split="val",
            question_id="1",
            question="what is the date?",
            image_path="a.png",
            answers=["1/8/93"],
            question_types=["form"],
        ),
        DocumentSample(
            dataset_name="docvqa",
            split="val",
            question_id="2",
            question="what is the company name?",
            image_path="b.png",
            answers=["ITC Limited"],
            question_types=["layout"],
        ),
    ]

    per_sample = [
        SampleEvalResult(
            question_id="1",
            question="what is the date?",
            prediction="1/8/93",
            answers=["1/8/93"],
            exact_match=1.0,
            anls=1.0,
        ),
        SampleEvalResult(
            question_id="2",
            question="what is the company name?",
            prediction="ITC Limited REPORT AND ACCOUNTS 2013",
            answers=["ITC Limited"],
            exact_match=0.0,
            anls=0.6,
        ),
    ]

    errors = collect_error_cases(samples, per_sample)
    assert len(errors) == 1
    assert errors[0].question_id == "2"
    assert "layout" in errors[0].question_types
```

# 四、现在怎么运行
先跑测试：

```bash
pytest tests/test_analysis.py
pytest
```

然后跑分析脚本：

```bash
python scripts/analyze_docvqa_baseline.py \
  --docvqa-root datasets/docvqa \
  --split val \
  --predictions-path outputs/preds/docvqa_val_ocr_baseline.json \
  --limit 50 \
  --num-errors 20 \
  --save-analysis
```

如果你接下来跑的是 300 条或 1000 条，也把 `--limit` 改成对应值。

---

# 五、这个脚本跑完后你会得到什么
你会拿到 3 类信息：

## 1. 总体指标
就是你之前已经看到的：

+ exact match
+ anls
+ 缺失预测数

## 2. 按 `question_types` 的分组指标
这很重要，因为你很快就能看到：

+ `layout` 类是否更难
+ `handwritten` 类是否更差
+ `form` 类是否相对容易

这能帮助你判断：

+ 现在规则更适合什么题
+ 以后要优先改哪类问题

## 3. 错误样例
这一步最关键。  
你会看到非常具体的错误：

+ 问题是什么
+ 正确答案是什么
+ 预测成了什么
+ 属于什么 question_types
+ 对应哪张图片、哪个 OCR 文件

这会直接指导你 baseline v2 的设计。

---

# 六、接下来该做什么
我给你一个很明确的优先级。

---

## 第一步：先跑这个分析脚本
这是你现在最值得做的。  
因为你不能在不知道错误分布的情况下瞎改规则。

---

## 第二步：根据错误分析做 baseline v2
你接下来大概率会看到下面几类问题：

### 问题 1：数值题返回成年份
比如你刚才那个：

+ 问的是 value per 1000
+ 结果返回了 `1975`

### 要怎么改
在 `ocr_retrieval.py` 里加：

+ 对含有 `value`、`amount`、`actual`、`per 1000`、`rate` 这类关键词的问题
+ 优先提取小数 / 数值
+ 并降低纯年份的优先级

---

### 问题 2：实体类问题返回整行太长
比如：

+ 正确是 `ITC Limited`
+ 预测成 `ITC Limited REPORT AND ACCOUNTS 2013`

### 要怎么改
加“短实体截断规则”：

+ 遇到 `company / university / corporation / person name` 这类问题
+ 如果候选行很长，优先截取前半段短实体
+ 去掉明显尾巴：
    - `REPORT`
    - `ACCOUNTS`
    - 年份
    - 一些固定噪声短语

---

### 问题 3：只看一行不够
### 要怎么改
从 “只选 top-1 行” 改成：

+ 选 top-3 行
+ 再选最可能答案的 span

---

## 第三步：再跑更大的 val 子集
当前你只跑了 50 条。下一步建议：

```bash
python -m mm_docvqa.inference.predict_docvqa_baseline \
  --docvqa-root datasets/docvqa \
  --split val \
  --limit 300 \
  --save-metrics
```

然后再跑分析脚本：

```bash
python scripts/analyze_docvqa_baseline.py \
  --docvqa-root datasets/docvqa \
  --split val \
  --predictions-path outputs/preds/docvqa_val_ocr_baseline.json \
  --limit 300 \
  --num-errors 30 \
  --save-analysis
```

只有样本数扩大一点，你看到的错误模式才更稳定。

---

## 第四步：开始记实验日志
你现在已经有 baseline v1 了，所以建议立刻建：

`docs/experiments.md`

你先写最简单的一版，内容包括：

+ baseline 名称：`ocr_baseline_v1`
+ 运行命令
+ 样本数：50
+ exact match：0.02
+ anls：0.03
+ 主要问题：
    - 数值题错得多
    - name/entity 类经常返回整行
    - 只看一行导致丢信息

以后每改一次规则，就加一条实验记录。

---

# 七、我建议你下一批最值得继续让我写的代码
等你跑完分析脚本以后，我建议下一批直接进入：

## baseline v2 改进
也就是继续改：

+ `src/mm_docvqa/baselines/ocr_retrieval.py`
+ `tests/test_baseline_docvqa.py`

我会帮你加：

1. 数值题抽取规则
2. entity/name 截断规则
3. top-k 候选行策略
4. 更细一点的问题意图识别

这样你很可能就能把 baseline 从“几乎不可用”提到“开始有一点像样”。

# 八、你现在马上该做什么
按这个顺序走：

1. 把上面 3 个文件放进去
2. 运行：

```bash
pytest tests/test_analysis.py
pytest
```

3. 再运行：

```bash
python scripts/analyze_docvqa_baseline.py \
  --docvqa-root datasets/docvqa \
  --split val \
  --predictions-path outputs/preds/docvqa_val_ocr_baseline.json \
  --limit 50 \
  --num-errors 20 \
  --save-analysis
```

4. 把分析结果贴给我

然后我下一条就直接帮你写 **baseline v2 的改进代码**。

# 结果好像不太行
结果“看起来不太行”其实很正常，而且这份分析已经非常有价值了。  
你现在已经明确知道 **v1 baseline 的主要失败模式**：

1. **数值题**：抓到了年份，没抓到真正的数值  
例子：`0.28` 被预测成 `1975`
2. **实体类题**：找到了正确行，但不会把答案从整行里切出来  
例子：`ITC Limited` 被预测成 `ITC Limited REPORT AND ACCOUNTS 2013`
3. **location / where 类题**：能定位到相关实体，但不会抽出地点部分  
例子：`UNIVERSITY OF CALIFORNIA, SAN DIEGO` 应该抽成 `SAN DIEGO`
4. **表格/日程类题**：当前几乎全灭  
因为现在还是“按整页 OCR 行打分”，还没有表格结构意识

所以你现在最合适的下一步，不是立刻上训练模型，而是先做一个 **baseline v2**：

+ 保留现在的整体结构
+ 把 `ocr_retrieval.py` 升级
+ 补新的测试
+ 再跑一次 50 / 300 条对比

---

# 现在直接给你下一批代码
这次我建议你做两件事：

1. **直接替换**`src/mm_docvqa/baselines/ocr_retrieval.py`
2. **更新**`tests/test_baseline_docvqa.py`
3. **小改**`src/mm_docvqa/inference/predict_docvqa_baseline.py` 里的 method 名和默认输出文件名

---

## 一、替换 `src/mm_docvqa/baselines/ocr_retrieval.py`
这版是 **v2**，比 v1 多了这些能力：

+ 区分问题类型：date / time / number / subject / company / university / location / person / session
+ 不再只看 top-1 行，而是看 **top-k 候选行**
+ 对 `company / university / subject / location` 做专门抽取
+ 数值题优先抽小数/金额/数字，降低把年份当答案的概率
+ 对 URL、纯噪声行做惩罚

把整个文件替换成下面这版：

```python
from __future__ import annotations

import re
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Literal

from mm_docvqa.domain.schemas import OCRLine, OCRPage
from mm_docvqa.evaluation.normalize import normalize_text

AnswerType = Literal[
    "date",
    "time",
    "number",
    "subject",
    "company",
    "university",
    "location",
    "person",
    "session",
    "generic",
]

STOPWORDS = {
    "what",
    "is",
    "the",
    "a",
    "an",
    "of",
    "in",
    "this",
    "that",
    "who",
    "whose",
    "which",
    "when",
    "where",
    "how",
    "many",
    "mentioned",
    "letter",
    "document",
    "name",
    "given",
    "does",
    "do",
    "to",
    "for",
    "on",
    "and",
    "or",
    "are",
    "be",
    "cc",
    "during",
    "year",
    "value",
    "actual",
    "per",
}

DATE_PATTERNS = [
    r"\b\d{1,2}/\d{1,2}/\d{2,4}\b",
    r"\b\d{1,2}-\d{1,2}-\d{2,4}\b",
    r"\b(?:jan|feb|mar|apr|may|jun|jul|aug|sep|sept|oct|nov|dec)[a-z]*\s+\d{1,2},?\s+\d{2,4}\b",
]

TIME_PATTERNS = [
    r"\b\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:a\.?m\.?|p\.?m\.?)\b",
    r"\b\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:to|-)\s*\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:a\.?m\.?|p\.?m\.?)\b",
    r"\b\d{1,2}\.\d{2}\s*(?:to|-)\s*\d{1,2}\.\d{2}\s*(?:a\.?m\.?|p\.?m\.?)\b",
]

NUMBER_PATTERNS = [
    r"\$\s?\d[\d,]*(?:\.\d+)?",
    r"\b\d[\d,]*\.\d+\b",
    r"\b\d[\d,]*\b",
]

URL_PATTERN = re.compile(r"(https?://|www\.|\.edu/|\.com/|industrydocuments)", re.IGNORECASE)

TRAILING_NOISE_PATTERNS = [
    r"\breport and accounts\b.*$",
    r"\bannual report\b.*$",
    r"\bfor the year ended\b.*$",
    r"\bpage \d+\b.*$",
]


@dataclass(slots=True)
class LineCandidate:
    score: float
    line: OCRLine


def simple_tokenize(text: str) -> list[str]:
    text = normalize_text(text)
    return re.findall(r"[a-z0-9]+", text)


def question_keywords(question: str) -> set[str]:
    tokens = simple_tokenize(question)
    return {token for token in tokens if token not in STOPWORDS and len(token) > 1}


def infer_answer_type(question: str) -> AnswerType:
    q = normalize_text(question)

    if "date" in q:
        return "date"
    if "time" in q:
        return "time"
    if any(x in q for x in ["value", "amount", "how many", "how much", "committee strength", "actual", "per 1000"]):
        return "number"
    if "subject" in q:
        return "subject"
    if "university" in q:
        if "where" in q or "located" in q:
            return "location"
        return "university"
    if "company" in q or "corporation" in q:
        return "company"
    if "where" in q or "located" in q or "location address" in q:
        return "location"
    if any(x in q for x in ["who", "to whom", "contact person", "presiding", "name of foundation"]):
        return "person"
    if "session" in q:
        return "session"
    return "generic"


def question_hints(question: str) -> list[str]:
    q = normalize_text(question)
    hints: list[str] = []

    if "date" in q:
        hints.extend(["date", "dated"])
    if "subject" in q:
        hints.extend(["subject", "re:"])
    if "contact person" in q or "contact" in q:
        hints.extend(["contact", "attention", "attn"])
    if "signature" in q or "whose signature" in q:
        hints.extend(["signature", "signed"])
    if "cc" in q:
        hints.append("cc")
    if "company" in q or "corporation" in q:
        hints.extend(["company", "corporation", "limited", "ltd", "inc"])
    if "university" in q:
        hints.append("university")
    if "location address" in q or "located" in q:
        hints.extend(["address", "street", "road", "ave", "washington"])
    if "to whom" in q:
        hints.extend(["to:", "dear"])
    if "session" in q:
        hints.extend(["session", "meeting"])
    return hints


def extract_after_colon(text: str) -> str:
    if ":" not in text:
        return ""
    parts = text.split(":", maxsplit=1)
    if len(parts) != 2:
        return ""
    return parts[1].strip()


def find_all_matches(patterns: list[str], text: str) -> list[str]:
    matches: list[str] = []
    for pattern in patterns:
        for match in re.finditer(pattern, text, flags=re.IGNORECASE):
            matches.append(match.group(0).strip())
    return matches


def find_first_date(text: str) -> str:
    matches = find_all_matches(DATE_PATTERNS, normalize_text(text))
    return matches[0] if matches else ""


def find_first_time(text: str) -> str:
    matches = find_all_matches(TIME_PATTERNS, normalize_text(text))
    return matches[0] if matches else ""


def find_number_candidates(text: str) -> list[str]:
    candidates = find_all_matches(NUMBER_PATTERNS, normalize_text(text))
    cleaned: list[str] = []
    seen = set()
    for c in candidates:
        c = c.strip()
        if c and c not in seen:
            cleaned.append(c)
            seen.add(c)
    return cleaned


def extract_years_from_question(question: str) -> set[str]:
    return set(re.findall(r"\b(19\d{2}|20\d{2})\b", normalize_text(question)))


def strip_trailing_noise(text: str) -> str:
    result = text.strip()
    for pattern in TRAILING_NOISE_PATTERNS:
        result = re.sub(pattern, "", result, flags=re.IGNORECASE).strip()
    return result


def shorten_entity_like_line(text: str) -> str:
    """
    Try to shorten long entity lines like:
    'ITC Limited REPORT AND ACCOUNTS 2013' -> 'ITC Limited'
    """
    text = strip_trailing_noise(text)

    # Cut at common separators when the left part is likely the entity
    for sep in [" - ", " | ", " / "]:
        if sep in text:
            left = text.split(sep, maxsplit=1)[0].strip()
            if left:
                return left

    # Remove trailing year if line is very long
    text = re.sub(r"\b(19\d{2}|20\d{2})\b$", "", text).strip()

    # If the line contains common report boilerplate, cut before it
    report_markers = ["REPORT", "ACCOUNTS", "ANNUAL", "FINANCIAL"]
    tokens = text.split()
    if any(marker in tokens for marker in report_markers):
        kept = []
        for token in tokens:
            if token.upper() in report_markers:
                break
            kept.append(token)
        if kept:
            return " ".join(kept).strip()

    return text.strip()


def extract_location_from_line(text: str) -> str:
    """
    Example:
    'UNIVERSITY OF CALIFORNIA, SAN DIEGO' -> 'SAN DIEGO'
    """
    text = strip_trailing_noise(text)

    if "," in text:
        parts = [part.strip() for part in text.split(",") if part.strip()]
        if parts:
            return parts[-1]

    value_after_colon = extract_after_colon(text)
    if value_after_colon:
        return value_after_colon

    return text.strip()


def extract_person_like_answer(text: str) -> str:
    text = strip_trailing_noise(text)
    value_after_colon = extract_after_colon(text)
    if value_after_colon:
        return value_after_colon
    return text.strip()


def extract_best_number(question: str, line_text: str, page_text: str = "") -> str:
    """
    Prefer decimal / money / short numeric values over the year repeated in the question.
    """
    q_years = extract_years_from_question(question)

    line_candidates = find_number_candidates(line_text)
    page_candidates = find_number_candidates(page_text) if page_text else []

    all_candidates = line_candidates + [c for c in page_candidates if c not in line_candidates]

    if not all_candidates:
        return ""

    # Prefer values that are NOT the year from the question
    non_year_candidates = [c for c in all_candidates if c not in q_years]

    # Prefer decimal or money-like candidates
    def rank_number(x: str) -> tuple[int, int]:
        has_decimal = 1 if "." in x else 0
        has_money = 1 if "$" in x else 0
        return (has_money + has_decimal, -len(x))

    preferred_pool = non_year_candidates if non_year_candidates else all_candidates
    preferred_pool = sorted(preferred_pool, key=rank_number, reverse=True)

    return preferred_pool[0]


def score_line(question: str, line: OCRLine) -> float:
    q_keywords = question_keywords(question)
    hints = question_hints(question)
    answer_type = infer_answer_type(question)

    line_norm = normalize_text(line.text)
    line_tokens = set(simple_tokenize(line.text))

    if not line_norm:
        return -10.0

    score = 0.0

    # Penalize noisy URL-like lines
    if URL_PATTERN.search(line.text):
        score -= 4.0

    # Basic keyword overlap
    score += float(len(q_keywords & line_tokens))

    # Hint bonus
    for hint in hints:
        if hint in line_norm:
            score += 2.0

    # Answer-type-aware bonuses
    if answer_type == "date" and find_first_date(line.text):
        score += 4.0

    if answer_type == "time" and find_first_time(line.text):
        score += 4.0

    if answer_type == "number":
        nums = find_number_candidates(line.text)
        if nums:
            score += 3.0
            # Penalize pure year-only line for number questions
            if all(re.fullmatch(r"(19\d{2}|20\d{2})", n) for n in nums):
                score -= 2.0

    if answer_type == "subject" and ("subject" in line_norm or "re:" in line_norm):
        score += 4.0

    if answer_type == "company" and any(k in line_norm for k in ["limited", "ltd", "corporation", "company", "inc"]):
        score += 3.0

    if answer_type == "university" and "university" in line_norm:
        score += 3.0

    if answer_type == "location" and ("," in line.text or "address" in line_norm):
        score += 2.0

    if answer_type == "person" and (":" in line.text or "dear" in line_norm or "to" == line_norm[:2]):
        score += 1.5

    if answer_type == "session":
        if find_first_time(line.text):
            score += 2.0
        if "session" in line_norm or "meeting" in line_norm:
            score += 1.5

    if ":" in line.text:
        score += 0.5

    # Slight penalty for overly long lines
    if len(line.text) > 120:
        score -= 0.5

    return score


def select_candidate_lines(question: str, ocr_page: OCRPage | None, top_k: int = 3) -> list[OCRLine]:
    if ocr_page is None or not ocr_page.lines:
        return []

    scored_lines = [LineCandidate(score=score_line(question, line), line=line) for line in ocr_page.lines]
    scored_lines.sort(key=lambda x: x.score, reverse=True)

    candidates = [item.line for item in scored_lines[:top_k] if item.score > -10]
    return candidates


def extract_answer_from_candidates(question: str, candidate_lines: list[OCRLine], page_text: str = "") -> str:
    q = normalize_text(question)
    answer_type = infer_answer_type(question)

    if not candidate_lines:
        return ""

    # Join top candidate texts for broader fallback search
    joined_candidates_text = "\n".join(line.text for line in candidate_lines)

    if answer_type == "date":
        for text in [joined_candidates_text, page_text]:
            value = find_first_date(text)
            if value:
                return value

    if answer_type == "time":
        for text in [joined_candidates_text, page_text]:
            value = find_first_time(text)
            if value:
                return value

    if answer_type == "number":
        value = extract_best_number(question, joined_candidates_text, page_text=page_text)
        if value:
            return value

    if answer_type == "subject":
        for line in candidate_lines:
            if "subject" in normalize_text(line.text) or "re:" in normalize_text(line.text):
                value = extract_after_colon(line.text)
                if value:
                    return value
        # fallback
        return strip_trailing_noise(candidate_lines[0].text)

    if answer_type == "company":
        best = candidate_lines[0].text
        return shorten_entity_like_line(best)

    if answer_type == "university":
        best = candidate_lines[0].text
        return shorten_entity_like_line(best)

    if answer_type == "location":
        best = candidate_lines[0].text
        return extract_location_from_line(best)

    if answer_type == "person":
        best = candidate_lines[0].text
        return extract_person_like_answer(best)

    if answer_type == "session":
        best = candidate_lines[0].text
        # if line contains time range, remove the time span and keep the session name
        time_value = find_first_time(best)
        if time_value:
            cleaned = re.sub(re.escape(time_value), "", best, flags=re.IGNORECASE).strip(" -:;,.")
            if cleaned:
                return cleaned
        return strip_trailing_noise(best)

    # generic fallback
    best = candidate_lines[0].text
    value_after_colon = extract_after_colon(best)
    if value_after_colon:
        return value_after_colon

    return strip_trailing_noise(best)


def predict_answer(question: str, ocr_page: OCRPage | None) -> str:
    """
    Baseline v2:
    1. infer answer type from question
    2. score OCR lines
    3. keep top-k candidate lines
    4. extract answer with answer-type-specific rules
    """
    if ocr_page is None:
        return ""

    candidate_lines = select_candidate_lines(question, ocr_page, top_k=3)
    if not candidate_lines:
        return ""

    return extract_answer_from_candidates(
        question=question,
        candidate_lines=candidate_lines,
        page_text=ocr_page.full_text(),
    )
```

## 二、更新 `tests/test_baseline_docvqa.py`
把这个文件替换成下面这版。  
这版比之前多测了：

```python
from mm_docvqa.baselines.ocr_retrieval import (
    extract_after_colon,
    extract_location_from_line,
    find_first_date,
    find_first_time,
    infer_answer_type,
    predict_answer,
    question_keywords,
    select_candidate_lines,
    shorten_entity_like_line,
)
from mm_docvqa.domain.schemas import BBox, OCRLine, OCRPage, OCRWord


def make_line(text: str) -> OCRLine:
    return OCRLine(
        text=text,
        bbox=BBox(0, 0, 100, 20),
        words=[OCRWord(text=token, bbox=BBox(0, 0, 10, 10)) for token in text.split()],
    )


def make_page(lines: list[str]) -> OCRPage:
    return OCRPage(
        page_no=1,
        width=1000,
        height=1400,
        unit="pixel",
        orientation=0.0,
        status="Succeeded",
        source="microsoft_ocr",
        lines=[make_line(text) for text in lines],
    )


def test_question_keywords() -> None:
    q = "what is the date mentioned in this letter?"
    keywords = question_keywords(q)
    assert "date" in keywords
    assert "what" not in keywords
    assert "this" not in keywords


def test_infer_answer_type() -> None:
    assert infer_answer_type("what is the date mentioned in this letter?") == "date"
    assert infer_answer_type("What is the subject of this letter?") == "subject"
    assert infer_answer_type("What is the name of the company?") == "company"
    assert infer_answer_type("Where is the university located ?") == "location"


def test_extract_after_colon() -> None:
    text = "Subject: Review of existing Brainstorming Ideas/483"
    value = extract_after_colon(text)
    assert value == "Review of existing Brainstorming Ideas/483"


def test_find_first_date() -> None:
    text = "Date: 1/8/93"
    assert find_first_date(text) == "1/8/93"


def test_find_first_time() -> None:
    text = "Coffee Break 11:14 to 11:39 a.m."
    assert "11:14" in find_first_time(text)


def test_shorten_entity_like_line() -> None:
    text = "ITC Limited REPORT AND ACCOUNTS 2013"
    assert shorten_entity_like_line(text) == "ITC Limited"


def test_extract_location_from_line() -> None:
    text = "UNIVERSITY OF CALIFORNIA, SAN DIEGO"
    assert extract_location_from_line(text) == "SAN DIEGO"


def test_select_candidate_lines_for_subject_question() -> None:
    page = make_page(
        [
            "Confidential",
            "Date: 1/8/93",
            "Subject: Review of existing Brainstorming Ideas/483",
        ]
    )

    candidates = select_candidate_lines("what is the subject of this letter?", page, top_k=3)
    assert len(candidates) >= 1
    assert any("Subject" in line.text for line in candidates)


def test_predict_answer_for_date_question() -> None:
    page = make_page(
        [
            "Confidential",
            "Date: 1/8/93",
            "RJRT PR APPROVAL",
        ]
    )

    prediction = predict_answer("what is the date mentioned in this letter?", page)
    assert prediction == "1/8/93"


def test_predict_answer_for_subject_question() -> None:
    page = make_page(
        [
            "Confidential",
            "Subject: Review of existing Brainstorming Ideas/483",
        ]
    )

    prediction = predict_answer("what is the subject of this letter?", page)
    assert prediction == "Review of existing Brainstorming Ideas/483"


def test_predict_answer_for_company_name_cleanup() -> None:
    page = make_page(
        [
            "ITC Limited REPORT AND ACCOUNTS 2013",
            "Some other line",
        ]
    )

    prediction = predict_answer("What is the name of the company?", page)
    assert prediction == "ITC Limited"


def test_predict_answer_for_location() -> None:
    page = make_page(
        [
            "UNIVERSITY OF CALIFORNIA, SAN DIEGO",
            "Some footer text",
        ]
    )

    prediction = predict_answer("Where is the university located ?", page)
    assert prediction == "SAN DIEGO"


def test_predict_answer_for_number_question() -> None:
    page = make_page(
        [
            "Year 1975 actual value per 1000 is 0.28",
            "Another line with 1975 only",
        ]
    )

    prediction = predict_answer(
        "What is the actual value per 1000, during the year 1975?",
        page,
    )
    assert prediction == "0.28"


def test_predict_answer_with_empty_ocr() -> None:
    assert predict_answer("what is the date?", None) == ""


def test_predict_answer_session_fallback() -> None:
    page = make_page(
        [
            "2.00 to 5.00 p.m. TRRF Scientific Advisory Council Meeting",
        ]
    )

    prediction = predict_answer("What session is at 2.00 to 5.00p.m.?", page)
    assert "TRRF" in prediction or "Scientific Advisory Council Meeting" in prediction
```

尤其你分析里已经看到：

+ `table/list`
+ `Image/Photo`
+ `figure/diagram`
+ `layout`

这些类别，本来就不是“单行 OCR + 规则”能解决好的。

所以你的项目接下来会自然分成两条路：

## 路线 A：把 OCR baseline 再做一轮小增强
比如：

+ top-k line 改成 top-k + 邻近行
+ 表格题加简单行邻接规则
+ 时间表问题做“时间匹配 + 取同一行后半段”

这是为了让 baseline 更像样一点。

## 路线 B：开始准备训练版
也就是后面做：

+ `docvqa_preprocess.py`
+ `train_docvqa.py`
+ `eval_docvqa.py`

也就是说，你当前 baseline 的真正意义，不是追高分，而是：

+ 打通链路
+ 明确错误类型
+ 为训练版提供对照组

# 报了如下错误该怎么解决？
(mm-docvqa-py311) wenjing@wenjing-Z790M-AORUS-ELITE-AX-ICE:~/文档/doc-multimodal-vqa$ pytest tests/test_baseline_docvqa.py

....F..........                                                                                                   [100%]

======================================================= FAILURES ========================================================

_________________________________________________ test_find_first_time __________________________________________________



    def test_find_first_time() -> None:
    
        text = "Coffee Break 11:14 to 11:39 a.m."

>       assert "11:14" in find_first_time(text)

E       AssertionError: assert '11:14' in '11:39 a.m'

E        +  where '11:39 a.m' = find_first_time('Coffee Break 11:14 to 11:39 a.m.')



tests/test_baseline_docvqa.py:64: AssertionError

================================================ short test summary info ================================================

FAILED tests/test_baseline_docvqa.py::test_find_first_time - AssertionError: assert '11:14' in '11:39 a.m'

1 failed, 14 passed in 0.03s

这个报错不是大问题，原因很明确：

你的 `find_first_time()` 现在会先匹配到 **单个时间**，所以它在这句：

```plain
Coffee Break 11:14 to 11:39 a.m.
```

里先拿到了后半段的：

```plain
11:39 a.m
```

而不是你想要的整段时间范围：

```plain
11:14 to 11:39 a.m.
```

---

# 为什么会这样
你现在 `TIME_PATTERNS` 的顺序大概率是类似这样的：

```python
TIME_PATTERNS = [
    r"\b\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:a\.?m\.?|p\.?m\.?)\b",
    r"\b\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:to|-)\s*\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:a\.?m\.?|p\.?m\.?)\b",
    ...
]
```

第一条规则是“匹配单个时间”，所以它会先在字符串里匹配到：

```plain
11:39 a.m
```

然后 `find_first_time()` 直接返回第一个匹配结果，于是测试失败。

---

# 最直接的修法
## 方案一：把“时间范围”规则放到前面
把 `TIME_PATTERNS` 改成这样：

```python
TIME_PATTERNS = [
    r"\b\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:to|-)\s*\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:a\.?m\.?|p\.?m\.?)\b",
    r"\b\d{1,2}\.\d{2}\s*(?:to|-)\s*\d{1,2}\.\d{2}\s*(?:a\.?m\.?|p\.?m\.?)\b",
    r"\b\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:a\.?m\.?|p\.?m\.?)\b",
]
```

意思是：

1. 先找“时间范围”
2. 再找“单个时间”

这样它就会优先匹配：

```plain
11:14 to 11:39 a.m.
```

---

## 方案二：返回“最长匹配”
这个更稳，我更推荐。  
因为“时间范围”通常比“单个时间”更长，你可以在 `find_first_time()` 里优先返回最长的那个。

把原来的：

```python
def find_first_time(text: str) -> str:
    matches = find_all_matches(TIME_PATTERNS, normalize_text(text))
    return matches[0] if matches else ""
```

改成：

```python
def find_first_time(text: str) -> str:
    matches = find_all_matches(TIME_PATTERNS, normalize_text(text))
    if not matches:
        return ""

    matches = sorted(matches, key=len, reverse=True)
    return matches[0]
```

---

# 我建议你怎么改
最稳的是：

## 同时做这两件事
1. 把 `TIME_PATTERNS` 里“范围模式”放前面
2. `find_first_time()` 改成返回最长匹配

---

# 你直接替换成这版就行
在 `ocr_retrieval.py` 里把时间相关部分改成：

```python
TIME_PATTERNS = [
    r"\b\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:to|-)\s*\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:a\.?m\.?|p\.?m\.?)\b",
    r"\b\d{1,2}\.\d{2}\s*(?:to|-)\s*\d{1,2}\.\d{2}\s*(?:a\.?m\.?|p\.?m\.?)\b",
    r"\b\d{1,2}[:.]\d{2}\s*(?:a\.?m\.?|p\.?m\.?)\b",
]


def find_first_time(text: str) -> str:
    matches = find_all_matches(TIME_PATTERNS, normalize_text(text))
    if not matches:
        return ""

    matches = sorted(matches, key=len, reverse=True)
    return matches[0]
```

---

```

如果这个问题修好了，这条测试：

    assert "11:14" in find_first_time(text)
```

就应该能过。
